<# Important Notes (Category: ClanRaid)                                                                          |
    This API is called, if its not already cached, when a player opens their guilds Asguard logs menu. This
API specifically is a record of how much points each guild member contributed to the overall guild moral. I
do not currently see a strong need to track this information.

This API is Exportable: No

Long Term goals (Out of Scope of this project)
    N/A

Note for extension developer
 1.

#>

# Request
{
    "calls": [
        {
            "name": "clanRaid_logNodes",
            "args": {},
            "ident": "group_1_body"
        }
    ]
}
